The Inauguration of the Class B Union Yesterday Also Held the First Uprising Memorial Meeting of the Premier 99

The Second All-Line Representative Assembly of the Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Workers' Union of this line was held yesterday morning. As this day was the anniversary of the Premier's First Uprising, the Special Party Branch of the railway first held a memorial meeting for the Premier's First Uprising. Among those who signed in were Central Representative Wu Lanxi, Ministry of Railways Representative Han Jingyuan, Executive Committee members Chen Chengshi, Li Dasan, Song Chuanji, Feng Qihua, and Wang Weixia from the Special Party Branches of both lines, Secretary Xie Chengyu, Railway Bureau Director Huang Boqiao, Deputy Director Wu Shaozeng, Police Chief Ma Shaoping, Heads of various departments and sections, Representative Zhao Yu, and others, totaling ninety-six people, as well as all staff members of the assembly secretariat, and representatives and guests from various organizations such as Zhou Xuexiang, Lu Kepeng, and Wang Yalen, totaling over three hundred people. The proceedings of the meeting are recorded below:

Premier's Uprising Commemoration

The Premier's First Uprising Commemoration Meeting was opened, chaired by Chen Chengshi, Standing Committee Member of the Party Branches of both lines. After the meeting was opened according to protocol, a report was immediately made on the events of the Premier's First Uprising and the significance of the commemoration, roughly as follows: "The Premier launched an uprising in Guangzhou on September 9th, seventeen years before the founding of the Republic of China, but it tragically failed due to improper handling of weapons. Martyrs such as Lu Haodong, Qiu Si, and Zhu Guiquan sacrificed their lives. The Premier went to Japan with Zheng Shiliang. This was the Premier's First Uprising. We are holding this commemoration today, coinciding with the tenth anniversary of the Premier's passing, at a time when the nation is facing difficulties, with natural disasters and man-made calamities pressing down upon us. We should invigorate the spirit of the Party, strive to save the nation from its current plight, deeply reflect on ourselves, uphold the Premier's legacy, strive for the well-being of our Party comrades, boost the revolutionary spirit, and overcome the current national crisis."

Opening of the Representative Assembly

At 9:20 AM, the opening ceremony was held, chaired by Zhao Yu, Cai Wanquan, Wu Renfu, Yao Xiaojiang, Hong Desheng, and four others. Wu Renfu and Zhao Yu served as chairmen, Wang Cheng and Tang Xiongjie as recorders, and Huang Rui as the master of ceremonies. After opening the meeting according to protocol, Chairman Wu Renfu respectfully read the Premier's will.

The Chairman's Opening Address was followed by the opening address of Chairman Zhao Yu, which stated roughly as follows: "Today, our railway union is holding its Second All-Line Representative Assembly, which is of extraordinary significance. Looking back at the First Assembly of our railway union, its organizational members included clerks and staff, which was inconsistent with the Trade Union Law, and it was never officially registered. The organization was not perfect, so the higher-level Party branch presented a request to the Central Committee to send personnel to carry out reorganization, which has now been over half a year. With the guidance and supervision of the higher-level Party branch and the Railway Bureau, and the efforts of the instructors and reorganizers, after actively implementing the reorganization, we are able to formally hold the opening ceremony of the Second All-Line Representative Assembly today. We feel infinite joy and hope. We should pool our efforts to provide a place for over ten thousand railway workers to rely on and follow, and with one heart and one mind, the future is bright. How can we ensure the permanent health of the two railway unions? This requires the careful and thorough consideration and active efforts of all representatives, and we hope that the Central Committee, the Ministry, and the officials of the Party branch and the Railway Bureau will provide guidance and support."

Instructions from the Central Representative were given by Central Representative Wu Lanxi, roughly as follows: "Comrade workers, today I am honored to participate in your grand ceremony on behalf of the Central Committee, and I feel infinite joy and honor. In this time of national crisis, I would like to offer two suggestions to all of you for our joint efforts: (1) To enhance national consciousness and jointly seek the independence, freedom, and equality of our Chinese nation; (2) When we do things, we should focus on the big picture and start with the small details. We should always use this as a principle, no matter what we do; (3) To increase national production and strengthen national power. During this national crisis, all domestic industries are lagging behind. We should accomplish two days' work in one day's time, work hard, and catch up. Only then can our nation be revived."

Instructions from the Representative of the Ministry of Railways

Instructions were given by Han Jingyuan, Representative of the Ministry of Railways, roughly as follows: “According to the regulations of the Trade Union Law, railway workers must hold a representative assembly once a year. However, the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Workers' Unions have not held a second assembly as scheduled since the first representative assembly in September 1931, after four years, due to various reasons. Now, through the efforts of the comrades of the special party branches of the two lines, the responsible personnel of the railway bureau, and all the representatives, and after a long period of reorganization, the second representative assembly can be convened today, and the difficulty of the process is even more commendable. I am deeply honored to participate in this precious gathering on behalf of the Ministry of Railways. The two lines connect the political center of the country, the capital, and the economic center, Shanghai, and their importance is the highest in the country. Therefore, the development of the two lines is of great importance to the country's political and economic relations. If we want to promote the development of railway business, there are two necessary conditions: one is material conditions, and the other is human conditions. Comparing the two, the latter is more important than the former. Because under the same material conditions, whether people do their best is enough to influence the entire cause. The sages said, ‘It is up to people to make things happen,’ and ‘Man can conquer nature.’ The railway staff is the largest number of workers, so in other words, among the human conditions, the most important thing is the efforts of the workers. If the workers want to work hard, the first step must be a sound organization, that is, a sound trade union. The Second Representative Assembly of the two railway unions is held today, and its organization is indeed sounder than the first one. With this sound trade union, it is expected that the future of the road will gradually develop and make great strides forward."

Instructions from the Representative of the Party Branch

Li Dasan, Standing Committee member of the Party branches of both lines, gave instructions, stating roughly as follows: "In the past, the trade union of this line was unable to develop its work due to its unsound organization. The special party branch of this line, in view of this, in order to ensure the purity of the members and strictly abide by the organization of the Trade Union Law, ordered the trade union to stop its activities and sent personnel to reorganize it, in accordance with the instructions of the Central Committee. After a long period of efforts by the reorganizers and instructors, the Second Representative Assembly can be held today. The speaker, on behalf of the special party branch of this line, feels very happy to participate in the grand meeting. Our country's production is backward, the rural areas are bankrupt, the society is in depression, and all construction is still undeveloped. In addition, foreign aggression has been frequent over the years. In every way, it is enough to show that the Republic of China has reached an extremely dangerous period. In this period, we can only work together to save the crisis. The two trade unions of our line also bear considerable responsibility. Furthermore, as the railway is an important cause of national construction, the railway workers should take national prosperity as a prerequisite and cannot always seek comfort for themselves. The two railway unions have not seemed to pay attention to this point in the past, so I would like to raise this point in the hope that you will not only pay close attention to it, but also tell all the workers of this line."

Instructions from the Director of the Railway Bureau

Huang Boqiao, Director of the Bureau, gave instructions, which were solemn and important. They are recorded as follows: "(1) There must be a legitimate organization, and it must be handled in accordance with the legal procedures so that the railway union can exist permanently and seek benefits for all the workers. (2) There must be legitimate work, and everything must be done according to the rules, for the sake of the public, and with consideration for laws and regulations. (3) I hope that the workers will thoroughly understand the relationship between the state-owned railway and the workers. (4) I hope that the workers will thoroughly understand production and construction. (5) I hope that the workers will understand traffic mobilization. (6) I hope that the workers will understand the current economic difficulties of this line. (7) I hope that the trade union will lead all the workers to overcome this difficulty together with the railway bureau. Finally, I would like to encourage all the representatives with three common sayings: 1. The meaning of 'a rising tide lifts all boats.' 2. 'You must feed the sheep well before you can get wool.' 3. 'If you want to eat eggs, you must feed the hen well.' After that, Wang Yalen, representative of the special party branch of the Shanhaiguan Railway Bureau, gave a speech, which is not recorded due to its length.

Chairman's Reply

Finally, Chairman Wu Renfu gave a reply, stating roughly as follows: "The trade union of this line is holding its Second Representative Assembly today. We are very honored to have the representatives of the Central Committee, the Ministry of Railways, the special party branch, the Railway Bureau, as well as the reorganizers and instructors present to guide us. We will accept all the instructions from you with 120,000 points of sincerity and do our best. In the past, the organization of the two railway unions was not perfect and the members were too complex, just like farmers sowing seeds that were not pure, so the results were often not satisfactory. Now, with the assistance of the special party branch, the Railway Bureau, and all parties, we have picked out all kinds of impure elements one by one and replanted them, so we can convene the Second Representative Assembly today. In addition to encouraging ourselves to cooperate, on the other hand, we hope that the Central Committee, the Ministry of Railways, the special party branch, the Railway Bureau, and all the guests can continue to give us instructions at any time, as a compass, and please continue to give us assistance at all times, so that the seeds sown today can gradually flourish. It is our sincere hope.” Then, slogans were shouted and a group photo was taken, marking the completion of the ceremony. It is reported that the first meeting will continue at 3:00 PM to pass the charter and elect supervisors and directors.

We express our gratitude to the Minister and declare that we are willing to respectfully obey the instructions of the Sacred Congregation. Cai Ning.

Mr. Blanc Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday from the Philippines Under Escort 103

The Da Mei Evening News reported that Mr. Blanc, the former vice president of the American Eastern Banking Corporation, has been handling the liquidation affairs of the branch established by Mr. Reaven in Manila. Because Mr. He Fu, the liquidator of the American Feng Bank, accused him of being involved in fraud with Mr. Reaven and others, he was detained by the Philippine authorities and handed over to the captain of the President Coolidge, who escorted him to Shanghai. He arrived in port today (the 9th). Because a certain American company had submitted a bond of US$10,000, he was able to disembark freely today. When asked about the accusations, he replied that he did not know the details.

Shanghai Branch of Guangdong Bank Ordered by Head Office to Liquidate; Guangdong Associations Telegraph Request for On-Site Liquidation 104

The Xin Xin News Agency reported that after the Shanghai branch of Guangdong Bank closed down, it followed the Ministry's order and reported the actual situation of its assets and liabilities to the Banking Association, which was forwarded to the Ministry of Finance. Because the branch's assets and liabilities offset each other and there was a surplus, there was once a widespread rumor that it would resume business. However, the branch received a telegram from its Hong Kong head office at 6:00 PM last night, deciding to liquidate and hiring British lawyer Mr. Halwarth as the liquidator. It is reported that Mr. Ha is scheduled to go to the bank at 9:00 AM this morning to implement the liquidation. After receiving the telegram, the branch manager Zhang Rongpu prepared all the account books and prepared to hand them over to the liquidator today for liquidation. Since the branch's assets and liabilities offset each other and there is a surplus, depositors will not suffer losses after the liquidation. The Guangdong Fellow Association in Shanghai, the Guangzhao Office, the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Federation, and other organizations believed that Guangdong merchants had suffered significant losses after the bank closed down. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to the Hong Kong Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, which was forwarded to the bank's board of directors, hoping that the Shanghai and Hankou branches would liquidate on-site. The original telegram is recorded as follows: To the distinguished gentlemen of the Hong Kong Chinese General Chamber of Commerce: According to the creditors, Yangzi Hotel, etc., please forward this to the board of directors of Guangdong Bank. The closure of the Shanghai and Hankou branches has caused great losses to Guangdong overseas Chinese. The Ministry of Finance and the Banking Association have promised to do their best to maintain it. Please withdraw the liquidator immediately and order the Shanghai and Hankou branches to liquidate on-site. The creditors in Shanghai have filed a criminal lawsuit. What do the directors think? Please reply by telegram.

Typhoid Bacteria Stolen and Recovered from National Shanghai Medical College; President Reported Theft and Stolen Goods Recovered; Indictment Filed, Rescheduled for Retrial 105

Lu Zuo, a youth named Zhou, 20 years old, from Zhuji, Zhejiang, worked as a biochemical technician at the National Shanghai Medical College at 373 Avenue Haig in the French Concession. He shared a dormitory with Zhou Futian, a fellow villager who worked as a bacteriology technician at the college. On the night of the 6th of this month, Zhou Futian accidentally forgot the key to the bacteriology department's room in the dormitory. Zhou Lu Zuo picked it up and hid it. That night, he secretly opened the door of the bacteriology department and stole a tube of typhoid bacteria, hiding it under the bed in the bedroom. Later, Zhou Futian discovered that the key had been stolen, and after realizing something was wrong, he reported it to the president, Dr. Yan Fuqing (55 years old, from Shanghai). Dr. Yan tried to open the door of the bacteriology department and found that a tube of typhoid bacteria was missing. Dr. Yan considered the lost bacteria to be a major matter. If it were to fall into the hands of outsiders, it would affect public health. He believed that Zhou Lu Zuo was highly suspicious. When he questioned him, he denied it outright. Yan then reported it to the Foch Police Station and requested an investigation. After investigation by detective Wang Ronggui and detective Yao Zhupo, Zhou Lu Zuo was arrested. After confessing the location where the bacteria were hidden, the stolen goods were recovered. Zhou Lu Zuo was taken into custody and escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court yesterday morning. Lawyer Fei Xizhen of the Police Department explained the case and requested a postponement, waiting for the investigation of the case before filing a lawsuit. The plaintiff, Yan Fuqing, also came to court to explain the theft of the bacteria and requested the withdrawal of the lawsuit. The court said that the police station had not yet filed a lawsuit and needed to wait for the investigation before the lawsuit could be withdrawn. When questioned, the defendant Zhou Lu Zuo admitted to stealing, aiming to study the causes of bacterial growth. The court asked that since he was in the medical college, he could ask to study, so why steal? The defendant was speechless and had no answer. After examination by judge Sun Pengxian, the hearing was rescheduled for the 11th, and the defendant was returned to custody.

Huang Xianyao and Others; The Case of Forging Documents Concluded; —Sentence Scheduled for the 16th— 106

Huang Xianyao, the second son of the late Huang Chu Jiu, founder of the Gongfa Company, Riyue Bank, and the Great World, colluded with lawyer Mi Jingshen and clerk Wu Jiajin, who are now working in other places, to defraud his father-in-law Zhou Songqing of money by forging a note of 100,000 yuan from Zhou. He filed a petition with the Shanghai District Court for mediation, but it was unsuccessful. Subsequently, Wang Shaozeng and other creditors of Gongfa Company learned of this and filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, accusing Huang Xianyao and Zhou Songqing of damaging creditors' rights. After being examined, he opened a safe deposit box at the Guohua Bank and took out the original note. Zhou immediately surrendered it to the French Police Station, accusing Huang Xianyao of forging documents. The self-litigation case on the creditor side was suspended as a result, pending the police station's investigation and indictment. Later, the police station identified the handwriting on the note as forgery and escorted Huang to the Second Special District Court to file a public prosecution. After repeated trials by Judge Li Changnian, the two defendants, Mi and Wu, were not present because they could not be summoned. The trial of Huang Xianyao had already been concluded, and a date was set for sentencing. However, the judge in charge of the case, for the sake of caution, revoked the conclusion of the debate and scheduled a new debate. All the details have been reported in the previous newspaper. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Judge Li of the Second Special District Court presided over the trial in the First Criminal Court and informed the defendant of the reasons for the new debate. After questioning, Huang Xianyao confessed that he had originally hired lawyer Mi Jingshen to handle the cohabitation case with his wife, and they took advantage of the opportunity to forge the note. After the application for mediation failed, he stopped the proceedings. Later, they offered the note to the creditors, resulting in a lawsuit. He was actually deceived and implicated, and the note was not forged by him. He had never threatened or extorted money from his father-in-law and requested that he be acquitted. After the questioning, the court ordered the debate to begin. After the police department lawyer Gu Shouxi and the defendant's defense lawyer debated each other, the court announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the sentencing for the 16th.

Demanding Deposits; Huang Jin Wrote a Threatening Letter; Resulted in Arrest and Detention Pending Trial 107

Huang Jinfu, the owner of the Jianhua Construction Factory at 51 Changping Road, Zhenjiang, had previously deposited 700 yuan in the Mingyao Commercial Savings Bank on Beijing Road. However, the bank announced its closure in May of this year due to the influence of its Qingdao head office. Several months have passed, and there is still no concrete solution for general depositors. The depositors have hired lawyers and filed lawsuits against the bank's responsible persons, Tong Jinhui and Yu Dehua, in the First Special District Court. The trials have been held several times, but have not yet concluded. However, Huang Jinfu had a different idea. On the afternoon of the 6th of this month, he wrote a threatening letter and delivered it to the home of Yu Dehua, the deputy manager of the Minghua Bank, at 19 Lane 640 Seymour Road, threatening to kill him if he did not return the deposit, saying that Yu's life would be in danger. After receiving the letter, Yu reported the situation to the Gordon Road Police Station, which dispatched Chinese Detective Zhu Mengwei to investigate. Until 7:30 AM the day before yesterday, Huang Jinfu suddenly wandered and peered at Yu's door, and was seen by two Chinese policemen, numbers 2099 and 2138, who found his behavior suspicious and arrested him. After Detective Zhu questioned him, Huang claimed that he was going to ask for the deposit. After the police compared the handwriting of the note written by Huang with the handwriting of the threatening letter received by Yu, they found that they were mostly similar. He was ordered to be detained and escorted to the Second Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Police lawyer Zhang Shizhu prosecuted him for the crime of intimidation under Article 305 of the Criminal Law. The defendant, Huang Jinfu, hired lawyer Jia Yaoxi to defend him in court. After a brief questioning by Judge Ye, he ordered that he be detained for a retrial in seven days.

螟蛉子顾中勋 控诉伪证案 顾纪生否认螟蛉 朱玄常全盘托出 —庭谕须调查前案案卷再审— 113

巳故前法捕房二号华探目，本地人，顾纪生，字紫祥，生前兼营地产起家，积资达数十万，在平济利路十四号，置有住宅一所，至年近花甲，尙抱伯道之忧，故螟蛤一子，名龙根，字唯一，成年为娶翁氏为媳，奈唯一沉溺黑籍，不事生产，又在外荒淫挥霍，顾悒悒不欢，乃于民国十九年间，拟再螟蛉一子，以望克绍箕裘，故托保镳曹和囡在外物色，会有苏乡孀陈袁氏之次子，有意过恋，经曹之说合，顾亦当意，遂于是年十月底，成立过继，由顾命寄子朱玄常，又名恩弟，（住马浪路一百七十六号）书立过继契约，双方各执，陈姓子遂入顾家为养子，时年十四岁，由顾为之取名顾中勋，讵知入门未久，因顾唯一为利害关系，坚持反对争吵，中勋遂不容于唯一，顾纪生恐日后肇成变故，乃将中勋寄养于住宅南首自产紫祥里看屋人顾根寳处，期年又被唯一得悉，家庭间波浪再起，顾又托其寄子朱玄常，将中勋领至望志路一五三号孔万昌家寄养，月贴饭金十二元，并送入通惠学校读书，至上年夏间，顾纪生亦忽食言停止给付中勋之饭食学费，存心遗弃，乃由中勋之生母陈袁氏，出面交涉无效，遂由陈袁氏以法定代理人资格，偕中动延律师具状特二法院刑庭，自诉顾纪生顾唯一父子遗弃，迭经传讯，顾否认螟蛉，又因要证朱玄常被顾方勾串，避不到案，一面具状声明否认代书过继契约终至陈袁氏母子控案驳回，虽经一再上诉均皆失败，兹陈袁氏与子顾中励以讼案之失败，皆被朱玄常一人受顾方敎唆，充作伪证所致，心不甘服，爰再延胡觉祝匡明两律师代理具状特二法院刑庭自诉朱玄常伪蹬罪，请依刑法一六八条讯办云云，法院据状，由王纲煦庭长一度传讯，被吿供认被顾方逼迫，否认写据，奉谕候改期调查前案卷宗再讯，已略誌报端，昨日下午三时，又奉特二院王庭长开庭续讯，自诉人除法定代理陈袁氏下乡不到，由顾中勋偕律师到案，被吿朱玄常亦准时到案，先据顾中勋供诉自诉意旨称，我控吿被吿因我过继与顾纪生为子时，由被吿书写字据，上年我因被遗弃，与顾家打官司，被吿做伪蹬，否认写字据，故控吿他云云，讯之被吿朱玄常供，过房爷顾纪生，为养子顾唯一吃鸦片不好，托保镳曹和囡介绍，领陈姓次子过门为养子，次日托我领过房娘到黄金大戏院隔壁李茂春课命馆算命，一无冲尅回家隔数日后，由陈姓方面交来过继据底稿，由曹交顾纪生，顾差人来叫我去吃夜饭，后令我照过继据稿子，誊写一式二张，次日由双方到塲签字，后来顾唯一得知反对，吵闹不休，由曹和囡与顾纪生商量，将新收养子，寄在自己住宅南面自己产业看屋人顾根寳处，不满一年，又被唯一知道，又吵起来，顾纪生恐被唯一害死，来遇我商量，寄养到孔家去，每月贴付饭钱十二元，并托我到通惠学校报名，亦由顾纪生起名字叫顾中勋，乃由我代去报名，送到学校读书，后来一年多，顾纪生不付饭钱，陈家起訢打官司，由顾纪生夫妇与顾唯一叫我去商量，命我具状声明，并令我撰状稿交管耀先律师办理，当时状稿写得不对，叫我重写，当初顾中勋过继时，陈家由好婆与阿叔到塲的等语，至此顾中勋声称，我还要控吿顾唯一笪耀先敎唆伪证，请求提案讯究官乃谕調査前案案卷，向高三分院调取，据复案卷在最高法院，尙未发回，讯顾中勋前案判决书可曾带来，顾答判决书在母亲处，我母帮佣，随主人下乡，下次可以到案，官乃谕改期九月二十三日再讯，并着自訢人下次须将前案判决书交案，以备参考，

Kerosene and Matches Not Accepted for Freight Collect 124

The Two-Roads Administration issued a notice yesterday stating that the Longhai Railway had inquired via telegram from various connecting railways whether they would handle kerosene, matches, etc., as freight collect, according to item 4 of section B of Article 2 of the "Responsible Transportation Regulations." After investigation, it was found that item 4 of section B of Article 2 of the "Responsible Transportation Regulations" stipulates that explosives and dangerous goods are not eligible for responsible transportation. However, kerosene, matches, fireworks, film, oilcloth, oiled paper, or their products are not subject to this restriction. Furthermore, Article 16 stipulates that all dangerous goods are not eligible for freight collect. Although kerosene and matches can be transported with responsibility, they are still considered dangerous goods and should not be eligible for freight collect. Therefore, the Administration has responded to the various connecting railways that freight collect will not be accepted. This notice is hereby issued for strict compliance.

Kaiming Bookstore Schedules Shareholders' Meeting 126

Kaiming Bookstore was founded in 1926 and reorganized as a limited company in 1929, having been in operation for six years. Its business has been quite successful. It is recently learned that the company has decided to hold its sixth annual shareholders' meeting at its general factory at No. 390 Wuzhou Road, Shanghai (south of O'Kai Road Bridge) at 2:00 PM on Sunday, October 13th. The meeting will report on the business situation of 1934, decide on profit distribution, re-elect directors and supervisors, and discuss important motions. If shareholders are unable to attend due to other commitments, they may entrust other shareholders to represent them. According to the company's articles of association, stock transfers will be suspended one month before the meeting. It is also learned that the company's capital increase of 150,000 yuan has been approved for registration by the Ministry of Industry, and new shares can be exchanged for receipts for stock payments.

"Xi Shi" Musical Drama to Be Performed Soon – A New Contribution from the Shanghai Theater This Autumn – Specially Made Magnificent Ancient Costumes and Grand Scenery 127

After the Shanghai Theater's performance of the drama "Modern Lady" at the Jincheng Theater this summer, its reputation soared. Major theaters in other cities vied to invite the troupe to perform, but all were politely declined. The main reason for this was to rush the rehearsal of Mr. Chen Dabei's musical drama "Xi Shi." It is said that Mr. Chen and director Gu Wenzong have rehearsed it to perfection. Once the Wanfang Troupe's engagement is over, it will be performed at the Carlton Theater. After that, it will travel to Beijing, Hangzhou, Pinghan, and other locations, performing both musical drama and spoken drama. The musical drama "Xi Shi" is divided into five acts, with songs and dances interspersed in each act. The songs include eight ancient melodies and folk songs such as "The Song of Guts and Gall," "The Song of Washing Silk," and "Nostalgia." These have been rushed into production as records by the Baidai Company and will be released soon. The dances include "The Dance of the Su Terrace," "The Dance of Washing Silk," and "The Dance of Gan Jiang," all wonderful ancient dances that had almost disappeared. These are the masterpieces of vocal expert Chen Gexin and dance expert Wu Xiaobang, who have exhausted their creative energies. The scenery includes magnificent sets such as "The Chang Le Palace," "The Gu Su Terrace," "The Echoing Corridor," and "The Washing Silk Stream." These were all designed and painted by art expert Hu Xuguang after personally visiting Suzhou and Zhuji to conduct on-site surveys. Shanghai residents will soon be able to enjoy a feast for the eyes and ears.

Letter to the Editor

To the Editor, In today's edition of your newspaper, on page two (tenth _), you published news about silk exports for August. Please note that the quantity mentioned is actually the export volume from August 16th to 31st. The total for the entire month was 6,981 bales, plus 2,467 bales of waste silk, totaling 9,448 bales. The year-to-date figure is 16,369 bales, plus 5,391 bales of waste silk, totaling 21,760 bales. To avoid any misunderstanding, we respectfully request a correction. Sincerely, Statistics Section, Silk Group. September 9th.

Weather Report

The Zikawei Observatory's weather forecast for 4:30 PM yesterday: Shandong and the surrounding areas are cloudy to clear, with strong northwest to northeast winds. There are cyclones and rain around Korea and southern Japan. The Yangtze River basin is clear and hot, with gentle northwest to southeast winds. The East China Sea has southwest to southeast winds. The hurricane will pass over the Sea of Japan, moving northeast by east. Its center was within about 60 miles of 36 degrees north latitude and 129 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM this afternoon. The wind force is unknown. Also, the highest temperature in Shanghai in the 24 hours before 1:00 PM yesterday was 95.4, and the lowest was 72.9. On the same day last year, the highest was 86.0, and the lowest was 64.8.

Spring and Autumn

Anecdotes 130

— (White-Necked Crow)

The ancients said, "Nothing in the world is more level than water." But water flows downward and only levels in a level place, showing that "levelness" is not water's inherent nature. It is also said, "Nothing in the world is more impartial than a mirror." But a mirror makes the beautiful more beautiful and the ugly uglier. People differ in beauty and ugliness, inherently an unfair creation. A mirror only knows to "reflect things as they are," unable to adjust in the slightest, correct the unfairness of creation, and make up for human defects. How can it be considered impartial? Therefore, there is simply no "fair" thing in the world.

When you are short of funds, you ask someone to lend you money, and they are very generous: "Hey! Feel free to borrow a few thousand or a few hundred yuan. Don't hesitate." And they readily agree. But when you are broke and want to borrow a dollar to pay the rent, you have to hem and haw and still can't get it out. If you manage to say it, you might get a cold laugh in return. It's not that people's attitudes are different; it's that your own position is different first. So the saying goes, "If you want to borrow eggs from someone, you must first raise a fat hen." This is also a very insightful life philosophy.

Female Teachers 131

— Bing Ding

I often think that if all the primary schools in the country used female teachers and became "mother schools," children's academic performance would definitely be more impressive than it is now. It's not that I'm infatuated with female teachers and dismiss male teachers altogether, but the facts proven by surveys and experience are enough to support my claim.

Children are the most adorable little angels, innocent and carefree. Women are calm, and men are lively. If given proper education, there is no reason why they can't succeed. The problem is that the teachers themselves are not yet successful, with shallow knowledge and bad behavior, and they spoil the good children they teach. Therefore, current teaching should not be about discussing doctrines and theories or coming up with new tricks but about strict certification of teachers. Then we parents can naturally rest assured about our children's education.

A dozen years ago, many female teachers were women who had problems in their marriages. Some had husbands who had affairs, causing rifts in their love; others were young widows who spent their time as primary school teachers to pass the years. Their situations were very pitiable. When I was a teacher at the XX Girls' School in N City, there was a Ms. B among my colleagues. She was gentle and effective in teaching, and the students were as affectionate to her as little birds. She had a daughter and a son whom she brought with her to study. They were intelligent, beautiful, and very lovable. A few days before the summer vacation of the following year, all the students suddenly learned that the principal had dismissed her and launched a farewell party as a memento. I sat in the audience and saw Ms. B take the stage. She first said a few humble words of encouragement and finally said, "Dear little brothers and sisters, thank you very much for holding a farewell party for me today. I hope that in the future, you will give me something that you may not refuse, right?" I was very surprised that she herself was asking the students for gifts. Unexpectedly, she continued, "Perhaps my dear little brothers and sisters would be willing to give me a few funeral couplets!" As she spoke, her eyes turned red. At this time, many students in the audience began to sob, and I felt a pang of sadness and ran outside.

It turned out that Ms. B's husband, although a scholar, was of bad character and willingly degraded himself. He had fallen into a state of depravity and was wandering outside all year round, and no one knew where he was. Ms. B was introduced by _ Jun to teach at the XX Girls' School in N City. The condition was that in addition to a monthly salary of twenty yuan, she would be exempt from tuition and board fees for her two children. Later, because the school's finances were strained, they had to dismiss her and hire a Ms. C, which saved the cost of feeding two children. But Ms. B's life became problematic because of this!

High Counter 132

— Zhou Xian

The most obvious difference between pawnshops and ordinary stores is the counter, which is at least twice as high as that of ordinary stores. _ is hidden high up, holding up a water pipe, with an utterly upright pawnbroker's face, overlooking everything outside the counter, making the anxious pawner standing outside the high counter seem three feet shorter.

Speaking of the high counter in pawnshops, it is incredibly imposing. I remember when I was little, I went to pawn something under strict orders. The counter was high, and I was short. I had to stand on my tiptoes, holding my breath, just to get the clothes package onto the counter. The pawnbroker glanced at the clothes package as if he didn't care, and coldly said, "Five yuan." But I was under strict orders to pawn it for eight yuan. The pawnbroker said with a stern face, "At most six yuan." As he spoke, he pushed the clothes package to the edge of the counter. But I stood on my tiptoes and couldn't reach it. So the pawnbroker pushed the clothes package casually, and it fell to the ground, scattering the clothes. On that occasion, I had an impression of this high counter that I would never forget.

But this arrogant high counter is said to be on the path to misfortune now. Every high counter only spits out white silver dollars, swallowing goods that are fully pawned but cannot be redeemed. Therefore, the pawnshop owners are at a loss. The pawnbrokers are also not as leisurely and carefree as before, holding up their water pipes all day long. The high counter, in form, is still squatting high, but its power is no longer what it used to be.

This year, Shanghai has seen many pawnshops close down due to the pressure of economic recession. In the interior, due to the collapse of the countryside, pawnshops are also closing down one after another. The few that remain are just eking out an existence. The golden age of the high counter has passed, and now it has reached the end of its rope. I am afraid that in the near future, the so-called "high counter" will become a historical term.

Little Western Paradise 133

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 18: Qi Party Makes Arrogant Advances, Flattering Petty Officials; Wife's Fierce Power Arises, Noisy Wife

As Ma San walked out, two attendants were already blocking the door, slapping him on the left and punching him on the right, knocking him back into the room. The two attendants followed closely behind, also entering the room. With stiff faces and upright torsos, they stood behind Ma San. Ma San thought that he had given Mrs. Lan a jab in the dark and that he could just turn around and leave. He didn't expect to be beaten back before he could leave the door. Turning back to see the two attendants, who were fierce and standing close, he had no choice but to stand still with his hands down. Commissioner Lan also sat up straight and said, "This thing is very hateful. We are talking to you here, why do you ignore us and turn around to leave?" Ma San had to lower his voice and said, "I thought there was nothing more to say, so I left. Because I only take care of the things downstairs." Commissioner Lan said, "I just want you to take care of the things downstairs. Listen, that crying woman is still sobbing. Go tell him that this Little Western Paradise is not rented by him alone. Tell him to be considerate of public morality and not to cry anymore. If he cries again, I will call the police." Ma San repeatedly agreed twice, but he didn't dare to move. Mrs. Lan said, "Go downstairs and tell him. If he cries again, I'll deal with you too. Get out!" Ma San slowly retreated out of the room, went down the stairs in a puff of smoke, and heard Yueying crying even harder in the room. He was about to open his mouth to speak inside, but he saw the door open, so he had to pause. At the same time, he heard Jia Duocai sigh and say, "Why don't you believe what I say? If I didn't think of you just coming to my side and using my temper, you wouldn't be able to stand it." He also heard Yueying say with sobs, "Think about it! My flesh and blood are telling me that my mother is sick, and you won't let me go back to see her. How can I not be sad?" (311)

Records of Lingering Fragrance 134

— Originally Written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

The eunuch tottered to hand a teaspoon of pearl powder to the Empress Dowager. As soon as the Empress Dowager took it, she stretched out her tongue and poured the powder into her mouth. At that time, we who were standing beside her had already prepared a cup of warm tea. As soon as she poured the pearl powder into her mouth, we hurriedly sent the tea over. She didn't take the teacup but drank a few sips from our hands, hurriedly swallowing the pearl powder.

"The amount of pearl powder is very important!" Once, she told me about the effects of taking pearl powder. "If you take a little bit, it can help us retain our youth. Its effect is purely revealed on the skin, which can make a person's skin always very smooth and radiant. Old people can be the same as young people. But the amount taken must be very small, and there must be a considerable amount of time between each time. If you eat too much or do not have a fixed time and eat it every few days, then it is not only useless to the human body but also greatly harmful!

Although she said that, I dare not say how sure I am that pearl powder has the effect of preserving beauty before we have experimented with it. Even if the Empress Dowager's appearance can be maintained to be more tender than ordinary old people, I cannot actually prove whether it is the result of regularly taking pearl powder. I only know that until I left the palace, the Empress Dowager's habit of taking pearl powder was never interrupted, and she always seemed to take this matter very seriously. (411)

A Little Fear of One's Wife Leads to Abundance 135

— Shijiu

"A little fear of one's wife leads to abundance." This saying is quite believable.

Dr. Mou's reputation has grown day by day since returning from abroad, and his career has unknowingly become more and more prosperous. His door is crowded during the day, and he has to go out for house calls in the afternoon. He is really a bit too busy. His family was not very wealthy, but since he hung up his shingle, in less than a few years, a Western-style house has been built in the city center. This is all thanks to his wife.

She is an old-fashioned woman, and he and she are not very compatible. However, the family's economic power is completely in her hands. He doesn't even know how much he owns, and his name is not on any bank savings accounts.

She is very meticulous and likes to be generous with small favors. Therefore, she knows exactly how many patients he sees each day, how many house calls he makes, and how much he charges for injections, down to the last penny. Sometimes, when she is happy, she gives him one or two yuan to spend, but he still has to report everything in detail, and only after it is approved can he get the money.

She is naturally very frugal in managing the family. Although she likes to play mahjong, she likes to think of it as a pastime and doesn't care about winning or losing. In the summer, when she gets happy playing mahjong, she delegates the bathing of the children to him. Sometimes, she finds the children troublesome, so she takes out a few dimes from the mahjong table and tells him to take the children to see a movie. Although he is not very willing to do these things when he is tired after bathing, he has no choice but to obey.

She often tells people, "Each of the three sons will build a Western-style house for him in the future." Dr. Mou feels a little unwilling to be a workhorse at first, but when he thinks of "a little fear of one's wife leads to abundance," he calms down.

Social Snapshots

That So-Called Accomplished One 136

— Pillow-Sun

A relative of mine, surnamed Mou, thanks to his father and grandfather's legacy, had a comfortable family life. He graduated from university and possessed some talent. During his school years, he would always flirt with girls, the so-called "loving widely but devoted to none." People excused him, assuming he wasn't mindful of the caution against being unrestrained in one's youthful ardor. After marrying, he didn't mind the stale formalities of the wedding ceremony, but he treated his bride quite fondly, and they had children. However, an extramarital affair gradually became known at home. Before long, he was bewitched by his mistress and promptly falsely accused his wife, abandoning her and their children. A new woman entered his house, also with children of her own. Then, he had another fling, quickly left her, and went to his new favorite. Now, Mou is approaching fifty. It's estimated that the number of extramarital affairs he's had is countless, and the offspring he's left in the world are truly numerous. Just recently, I heard that he has a new paramour. Alas, how prolific!

When Mou abandons his wife and children, even if his original wife is deeply attached and yearns for him, wanting to turn into a stone waiting for her husband, or others are left wandering on the crossroads, ultimately becoming flowers fallen into the latrine, he willingly plays the heartless Wang Kui, never once feeling a pang of pity or shame. As for those who wish to remain with him for a long time, he regards them like a widow who keeps to herself in memory of her deceased husband. I once happened to spend a night with a woman who lingered in a humble inn amidst the crowing of roosters, and she hastily departed before dawn under the waning moon, ensuring that her lovely eyebrows wouldn't be waiting for him. Or, if someone else plans to stay with him, he regards it as Luo Fu having her own husband after all. I once happened to secretly cross Chencang, enjoying the romance, so don't blame her for not marrying for ten years.

As for the children he had with their mothers and then left, he doesn't care about their food, clothing, education, or upbringing. Some can barely manage to stay with their mothers, while others are overwhelmed and the mothers and children are separated. He leaves them to drift like duckweed, struggling in the flow of fate, ultimately becoming heroes or villains, thieves or prisoners, or starving corpses and withered bones, just like the people of Qin viewing the thin or fat of the Yue people, remaining indifferent and unmoved! The ancients said, "Care for the young of your own, and extend that care to the young of others." What he practices can be twisted to mean, "This 'young' is mine, I care for my own and abandon the 'young' of others!" Thus, people know that he adheres to the principle of not recognizing goods after leaving the store.

Mou is certainly an intellectual. He chases after the delights of the world of beauty, neglecting his life, developing chronic illnesses, losing his wealth, and abandoning his career, to the point where people hardly acknowledge him. Yet, he eloquently justifies himself with philosophical and enlightened views: "Alas! People of the world toil their entire lives, exhausting their energy and spirits without hesitation. What are they after? Are they not merely seeking the joy of wives and children, and the desire to expand their family's fame? I can easily obtain what even immortals find difficult and sages cannot achieve. Wealth and status are like fleeting clouds to me. Am I not happily content, enjoying supreme bliss? Moreover, a person's life should be about enjoying oneself! My life is limited. If I don't seize the moment, forget myself and my ego, and use it to please myself, but instead fret and worry, only indulging in desires of love, anger, and lust, I'm wasting this short life. It's all in vain! If you are content with it, then so be it! Alas! This is the source of all suffering for living beings. How pitiful is that!"

Listening to his words, he seems to have reached a decisive conclusion. However, everyone, including his own father, considers him a disreputable man. His virtuous wives, guarding their chastity, also guard their children, and ultimately suffer because of him. Is he then a delusional man? Strange! Can that so-called accomplished one possibly be someone who only cares about their own well-being? Or will they spend their life in romantic abandon without regret? I will record this and observe!

Sports News

Sichuan Delegation Finalized for National Games: 60 Male and 14 Female Athletes to Depart Sichuan Before the 20th of This Month to Participate in Ten Events Including Track and Field (Men and Women) 137

(Chengdu Dispatch) Sichuan's sports have had special achievements in the past. For example, the promotion of military sports was second to none nationwide. However, because the leaders failed to deeply understand the relationship between sports and the nation and its people, they went astray, which is regrettable. In recent years, due to the banditry of the Red Army in Sichuan, the military was busy suppressing the communists, the political situation was unstable, and the people were restless. This sports issue gradually stagnated. Since the establishment of the provincial government this year and the entry of the Central Army into Sichuan, all issues are progressing day by day, and a new Sichuan is being built. After Mr. Yang Quanyu took charge of education, he showed great enthusiasm for promoting sports. Originally, a sports supervisor should have been appointed, but because there were already eight supervisors, due to the circumstances in the province, a letter was sent inviting (after arriving in the province, the provincial government appointed) sports expert Mr. Liu Shenzhan to serve as a compilation and review committee member of the Department of Education, effectively bearing the responsibility of sports supervisor. Mr. Liu originally donated funds to establish the Southwest Sports College in Sichuan, spending ten thousand on his family. Later, he took the lead in promoting military sports in the Twentieth Army, serving as the director of the sports department. In 1931, Mr. Liu left Sichuan for Beijing, where the National Sports Conference was held in 1932. Mr. Liu sent an urgent express telegram beforehand to appeal, which was quite insightful. Later, he was hired by the Ministry of Education as an expert member, and his proposals were very important. After the conference closed, Mr. Liu worked for the Xinmin Daily and China Daily in Nanjing, and co-edited the martial arts, sports, and military supplement with Mr. Cheng Dengke in China Daily, promoting new sports. Mr. Liu took over from Mr. Yang and left Beijing for Sichuan in June, arriving in the province on July 16th. Because the provincial government was being relocated at the time, it was extremely difficult to handle affairs.

Preliminary Selection Process

After the Department of Education received the notice from the Sixth National Games Organizing Committee, it immediately issued an order to hold a provincial preliminary selection on August 3rd, and ordered each county and city to prepare to participate. Mr. Liu was ordered to prepare for the provincial preliminary selection on July 20th. The first preparatory meeting was held on the 24th, with only ten days to prepare. After continuous and extremely hard preparations, the meeting was able to open as scheduled, and the conference proceeded extremely smoothly, which was unprecedented in Sichuan province's sports meets. A total of 39 units participated, with more than 370 male and female athletes. The closing ceremony was held on the 9th. The results were very ordinary, but the spirit was excellent. On the 2nd, the second plenary meeting of the preparatory committee was held. Chairman Liu reported on the progress of the conference, the various results, and discussed various important cases before announcing the end. Regarding the location for training the athletes, the Huaxi University Huamei Dormitory and Yude College in the south of the city were contacted in advance as dormitories for male and female athletes, and the Huaxi University sports field was used as a training ground for the athletes. The proposed events to participate in include men's track and field, all-around, soccer, basketball, tennis, martial arts, and women's track and field, basketball, and tennis, ten events in total. The results of men's and women's volleyball were also good, but due to limited funds, despite the volleyball team's several requests, it was ultimately not approved. The training period was one month, from August 19th to September 8th. In terms of curriculum, they get up at dawn for morning exercises. There are lectures from 8:00 to 11:00 a.m., a spiritual talk for one hour in the afternoon, and two hours of exercise training. There are also games after dinner. The training staff includes training director Liu Shenzhan, managers Xiang Zhijun (male) and Zhu Wenfang (female), and secretaries Huang Xixia, Zuo Jingxiu, and Yu Shenchang. Deng Deguang is the soccer coach, Yang Jiayin is the basketball coach, Cai Yiping is the field events coach, and Long Zecheng is the track events coach. Sixty male athletes and fourteen female athletes are being trained.

Overall Delegation

After the Sichuan athletes for the Sixth National Games were selected through the provincial preliminary selection, they gathered at Huaxi University in the southern suburbs of the city on August 18th for collective training. The male athletes lived in the Huamei Dormitory, and the female athletes lived in the Yude Dormitory, which were very close to each other. Every day, under the enthusiastic guidance of the coaches and the athletes' hard work, their results have improved. The management is completely militarized. Although the Huada sports field is not very suitable, the school is large, the air is fresh, and the scenery is beautiful. It is indeed the best among the available options and is suitable for athletes to live in. Every morning from 5:00 a.m. to 6:30 a.m. and every afternoon from 3:30 p.m. to 5:30 p.m. are the times for track and field and various ball sports training. The names of the coaches and trainees and the daily schedule are listed below separately.

(1) Coaches and Management Staff

Liu Shenzhan, training director; Cai Yiping, coach for men's and women's field events; Long Zecheng, coach for men's and women's track events; Deng Deguang, soccer coach; Yang Jiayin, coach for men's and women's basketball; Xiang Zhijun, male manager; Zhu Wenfang, female manager; Huang Xixia, Zhuang Jingxiu, and Yu Zhongchang, secretaries.

Liu Shenzhan's Remarks

According to what Director Liu Shenzhan told reporters, the purpose of promoting sports is not to go to the sports meet, and the purpose of going to the sports meet is not to win the championship. This is not because Sichuan's results are ordinary, so I make this argument. Therefore, during the training period, I focused on the spiritual aspect and had great expectations for the male and female athletes.

I want to lay the foundation for being a person and a warrior for the restoration and the nation in this short period of time. Although the goal is like this, the habits of the athletes are too ingrained, and I have not seen that a satisfactory result can be achieved immediately. As for my return to Sichuan this time, knowing that the responsibility is great, the difficulties are many, and the obstacles are numerous, I still strive forward, which is really a matter of responsibility. I have always been determined to disregard sacrifice and disregard success or failure, and only know how to work hard. Although there are more than forty sports colleagues and there are factions, there is really no faction. Because the colleagues are so scattered that they cannot form a faction, there is really no group of more than three people, and their wills are extremely incompatible. In such a situation, it is difficult to cooperate. This time, my personal return to Sichuan is to fully prepare for the provincial preliminary selection. All colleagues serve as staff members of the conference. After several conversations with me, they can understand the position that the country and the nation need, and the position that sports can make. The spirit of cooperation shown in the conference is highly praised by the community. This cannot but be said to be a turning point for Sichuan's sports. Finally, Director Liu said that because the Sichuan team is too far away, they will probably start their journey east on September 20th.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Orders Attention to the Qualifications of Vocational School Principals 157

(Nanjing Telegraph) The Ministry of Education orders all departments and bureaus that whether or not the principal of a vocational school is a suitable person is deeply related to the progress of vocational education. The Ministry has revised the vocational school regulations, and the qualifications of principals of junior and senior vocational schools have been clearly stipulated. In particular, it is important to note that the current school and the subject being studied must be of the same nature and have expertise. Principals should not only be responsible for administration but also pay close attention to teaching practice and school improvement. According to the statistics of vocational schools across the country in the past year, only 45% of the qualifications of vocational school principals in various provinces and cities are of the same nature as the school subjects they are teaching, and 55% are of different natures. This kind of undesirable phenomenon is a major reason why most vocational schools cannot develop healthily. In addition, the qualifications of principals of private vocational schools in various provinces are mostly non-compliant, and many only have administrative experience but no educational experience. Furthermore, most of the vocational courses attached to middle schools in many provinces and cities have not been set up as separate schools in accordance with the regulations, which is even more inconsistent with the regulations. It is hereby ordered that the department comply with the requirements to improve each. For current principals of public and private vocational schools who do not meet the qualifications, they should be gradually replaced. For the selection of principals of public schools in the future, the process must be handled carefully, and private schools should be strictly supervised and guided so that all public and private vocational school principals are qualified. The vocational courses attached to each middle school should be set up as separate schools in order to comply with the regulations and promote vocational education. The implementation plan should be reported to the Ministry for record.

Zhong Daozan Appointed to Inspect Vocational Education in Zhejiang and Shanghai 158

(Nanjing, 9th) The Ministry of Education has appointed Zhong Daozan to inspect vocational education in Zhejiang and Shanghai. Zhong is scheduled to depart within a week and is expected to complete the mission in about one and a half months.

(Nanjing, 9th) Based on the industrial categories and vocational school subject investigation forms filled out by various provinces and cities, the Ministry of Education believes that the industrial categories in various provinces and cities and the existing vocational subjects are not closely related. Nanyang English Leadership Government Holds Joint Examination for Overseas Chinese Schools; Held in Seven Locations Including Singapore and Malacca; The Reason is to Check the Level of Students in Each School 161

At the end of last year, it was once rumored that the local government of Nanyang English Leadership would hold a joint examination for overseas Chinese schools. Fortunately, it gradually subsided. However, the Shanghai Overseas Chinese Federation recently received a report from the Singapore Overseas Chinese Newspaper stating that the examination has been revived and will be held at the end of this year. The reason given is to check whether the level of students in each Chinese school is consistent and to provide students in each overseas Chinese school with an opportunity to observe each other. The reporter of Shenshi News Agency has recorded the details as follows: (1) The date of the examination is in early November, about ten days before the Chinese school examination. Although this date is not fixed, it is relatively reliable. (2) The examination locations will be in Singapore, Malacca, Seremban, Kuala Lumpur, Ipoh, Taiping, Penang, and other places, held simultaneously. (3) Examination methods: Chinese language, Chinese literature, arithmetic, history, and geography, with 50 points as the passing grade for each subject. Those who pass three subjects are considered qualified. All students in the junior high school, senior elementary school, and junior graduating classes of each school are required to participate in the examination. (4) Examination level: The standard used for the level is not limited to textbooks but is based on the curriculum standards promulgated by the Chinese government's Ministry of Education, and is adopted with consideration of local conditions. (5) All schools subsidized by the local government will be ordered to participate. However, in special circumstances, or if the distance from the examination location is too far to comply, they may request permission to be exempted from the relevant authorities. 2. Schools that are not subsidized by the government will be invited to participate, but attendance is not forced. (6) Purpose of the examination: 1. To check whether the level of students in each Chinese school is consistent. 2. To provide students in each Chinese school with an opportunity to observe each other. (7) Examination certificates: The Ministry of Education will issue certificates to students who pass the examination for use as proof of employment or transfer after leaving school. (8) Examination questions: The examination questions will be formulated and issued by the Ministry of Education. (9) Grading of examination papers: Examination papers will not be graded by outsiders, but will be undertaken by personnel from the Ministry of Education. (10) Announcement of results: The list of results will be announced before the start of school next spring. At that time, the number of students enrolled in each school, the number of students taking the examination, and the number of students passing will be announced at the same time to show the good results of each school for reference. (11) Not a graduation examination: Because the purpose of this examination is completely based on the sixth and tenth articles, each school must still conduct its own graduation examination. (12) No examination of elective subjects: The reason for not examining this subject is that the course allocations in Chinese schools in each continent are not consistent. Some lack physics, some lack chemistry, and sometimes both are missing, making it extremely difficult to formulate questions. Reiterate the previous order and notify all city schools to comply.

Shanghai Education Bureau Stipulates Methods for Students to Obtain School Supplies; Reiterates Previous Order and Notifies All City Schools to Comply 162

The Shanghai Education Bureau instructs all primary and secondary schools in the city that, in view of the fact that the fees collected from students for school supplies were not standardized and could not meet the needs, which not only affected the progress of studies but also caused parents to be suspicious, the bureau printed a sample of the student school supply receipt form, published in the 283rd issue of the Education Weekly, and ordered all schools to comply. It is hoped that young people from all walks of life will no longer purchase these books for reading.

Little Men (4) (1) 169

– Originally written by Ms. Louisa May Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

"I'm going for a walk; do you want to come?" Ned asked, trying to act nonchalant, but also very grateful for her silent sympathy, as he thought everyone would despise him as a bad egg.

"Yes, yes!" Little May ran to get her hat, feeling quite fortunate to be accompanied by an older boy today.

Others also saw them walking away, but no one followed them, which shows that boys are both dull and crude, and they seemed to instinctively feel that in times of difficulty, the kind and loving Little May was their most suitable friend.

"This walk was beneficial to Ned. When he returned, he was quieter than usual and looked happy again, wearing a garland of chrysanthemums, which his little companion had woven for him while he was lying on the grass telling her stories.

No one talked about the unfortunate event of that morning, but its impact may have been all the more lasting. Ned tried his best to improve, and he also received much help, not only in his earnest prayers to God but also in the patient care of that good friend in the world. His kind hand, whenever Ned touched it, never failed to remind him that this was someone who had been willing to endure pain for his sake.

Commercial News

Finance 170

Silver Bullion Continuously Contracts, Major Players Cover Short Positions, Gold Price Pierces the 90 Yuan Mark —Rebounding by 12.3 Yuan— 171

Yesterday, the gold market opened with foreign bank purchases. In a matter of moments, confidence returned, and the market rebounded immediately. Major players showed excitement and occasionally covered short positions. Silver bullion continuously contracted, leading to demand exceeding supply, piercing the 90 Yuan mark. Early morning overseas silver market saw British rises and American stability. Modest fluctuations occurred in Montreal forward silver prices. Exchange rates continued to contract. London spot gold rose by three pence, boosting market confidence. Pre-market trading opened and immediately rose to around 80 Yuan. Fuxing, Yongfu, Yu Ying, and Hengyu all advanced, rising to over 4 Yuan, later remaining flat. The Central Bank's listed price was announced, with the British rate flat and the American rate contracted. Customs gold units rose by three li. The standard gold price was listed again at 930.7 Yuan. Market confidence remained good, and the upward trend solidified. Major players busily purchased bars, gradually driving prices up. Banks traded with each other. HSBC listed prices, with both American and British rates stable. There was considerable struggle midway. Sassoon also came to square up positions, tightening the exchange market. Prices finally rose again. However, major players took advantage of the high prices to sell, and banks also sold off, hindering the rise. Soon after, a bank opened 210 bars, and major players suddenly bought heavily, boosting buying interest again. In addition, predictions indicated that silver bullion would contract by four annas, once approaching the 90 Yuan mark. Sellers became active at high prices, and the market stabilized again at noon. The afternoon market opened peacefully, and banks sold off somewhat, briefly shifting from strength to weakness. However, sellers continued to sell high, and many waited for a better price. A report from Bombay indicated a further contraction of one anna, further boosting major players' buying interest, piercing the 90 Yuan mark. Short positions were covered urgently. Rumors circulated that the mainland wanted to acquire US dollars. Major players continued to advance, and the market became even more firm at the end, continuing to rise after the close. Although the overall trend of the day was bullish, it was quite mediocre in the middle. The market conditions of the day are recorded below:

The morning opening was 884.2 Yuan, rebounding 4.8 Yuan from last Saturday. It then became 4.3 Yuan. Dada, Yifeng, Yongda, Decheng, and Chunyuan Yong sold bars, lowering the price to 3.5 Yuan. After the increase in debt, the demand for pig lead has sharply decreased. Although stocks are not high, the market price has stabilized, estimated at 16.30 to 16.40 yuan per picul.
